  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_91018a08-5f3c-43f0-9884-1b72ed07db9a'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer8574632898424857249">A Guerra pelos Sete Reinos continua sem tréguas ou misericórdia. Com um golpe negro mágico, Stannis afastou do seu caminho o irmão rival Renly, e agora nada o impede de conquistar Porto Real, pela força, com a sua frota.   <span id="freeText8574632898424857249" style="display:none">A Guerra pelos Sete Reinos continua sem tréguas ou misericórdia. Com um golpe negro mágico, Stannis afastou do seu caminho o irmão rival Renly, e agora nada o impede de conquistar Porto Real, pela força, com a sua frota. Mas Tyrion, eleito a Mão do Rei, tem outros planos e, embora todos o subestimem pela aparência, prepara com sangue frio a defesa da cidade e a confrontação com Stannis numa batalha que se adivinha sanguinária.<br /><br />No Norte, Winterfell encontra-se à beira do perigo e é alvo da cobiça dos Greyjoy, mas Bran nada consegue ver para além dos estranhos sonhos que o atormentam de noite e dia. Para lá da muralha, Jon oferece-se para acompanhar um grupo de batedores enviado para encontrar os selvagens, enquanto a principal força da Patrulha da Noite se fortifica junto às montanhas. Se quer sobreviver, Jon terá que aprender a ser tão cruel como a terra assombrada habitada pelos selvagens.<br /><br />Mais uma vez, George R. R. Martin consegue manter-nos agarrados até à última página. Personagens que amamos são mortas sem dó nem piedade, personagens que odiamos conseguem conquistar o nosso coração. De Arya a Sansa, de Robb a Daenerys, todos terão um papel fulcral neste fabuloso quarto volume de <i>As Crónicas de Gelo e Fogo</i>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8574632898424857249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText16074351718598468874" style="display:none">A Clash of Kings, George R.R. Martin<br /><br />A Clash of Kings is the second novel in A Song of Ice and Fire, an epic fantasy series by American author George R. R. Martin expected to consist of seven volumes. It was first published on 16 November 1998 in the United Kingdom. A Clash of Kings depicts the Seven Kingdoms of Westeros in civil war, while the Night's Watch mounts a reconnaissance to investigate the mysterious people known as wildlings. Meanwhile, Daenerys Targaryen continues her plan to reconquer the Seven Kingdoms.<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز سیزدهم ماه آوریل سال 2015 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: نبرد پادشاهان کتاب 1 از جلد 2 (نغمه آتش و یخ، #2)؛ نویسنده: جورج آر. آر. مارتین؛ مترجم: رویا خادم الرضا؛ مشخصات نشر: تهران، ویدا، 1391، در 629ص<br /><br />جلد یک: بازی تاج و تخت، شامل سه کتاب: کتابهای 1 و 2 و 3؛ <br />جلد دو: نبرد پادشاهان، شامل دو کتاب: کتابهای 1 و 2؛ <br />جلد سه: طوفان شمشیرها، شامل دو کتاب: کتابهای 1 و 2؛ <br />جلد چهار: جشنی برای کلاغ‌ها، شامل دو کتاب: کتابهای 1 و 2؛ <br />جلد پنج: رقص با اژدهاها، شامل سه کتاب: کتابهای 1 و 2 و 3؛<br /><br />کتاب نبرد پادشاهان، مجموعه ای دو جلدی و دومین عنوان از حماسه ی نغمه آتش و یخ، نوشته ی جرج آر.آر مارتین است که در سال 1998میلادی به چاپ رسید، زمان به هم ریخته است؛ تابستانِ دهساله ی صلح و فراوانی به سر آمده، و زمستانی سرد و کُشنده، همانند حیوانی درنده و زخم خورده، در حال نزدیک شدن است؛ دو رهبر بزرگ، لُرد ادارد استارک، و رابرت باراثیون، که چندین سال توانستند قدرت خود را در دوره ای از صلحِ تحمیل شده، حفظ کنند، اکنون جانشان را به خاطر خیانتهای اشراف، و درباریان از دست داده اند؛ حالا، آشوب و هرج و مرج سرزمین پادشاهی را دربرگرفته، چرا که مدعیان تخت آهنینِ پادشاهیِ هفت گانه، خود را آماده میکنند تا از طریق آشوب و جنگ، تکیه بر جایگاه قدرت بزنند؛<br /><br /> با آشکار شدن نشانه ای شوم در آسمان، شش گروه مختلف برای تصاحب سرزمینی چندپاره، دست به قدرت نمایی زده اند راب، پسر ادارد، خود را پادشاه شمال اعلام کرده است؛ در جنوب، جافری تنها نامِ یک پادشاه را یدک میکشد؛ هر دو برادر رابرت تلاش میکنند تا قدرت را به دست آورند، و در سرزمینی دوردست، ملکه ای در تبعید، مادر اژدهایان، همه چیز خود را به خطر میاندازد تا تنها دارایی ارزشمندش را از صحرایی سوزان و کُشنده، به سلامت بگذراند، و تخت آهنین را از آن خود کند؛ ا. شربیانی</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13040256618615885114"><i>(review in english below)</i><br/><br/>Adorei! <br/>O autor revelou-se particularmente brilhante nesta parte da história, na forma como os personagens evoluem, no desenrolar dos acontecimentos, no modo como consegue manter-nos absolutamente suspensos, sem saber exactamente se as coisas são o que parecem...<br/>Estive constantemente "agarrada", sempre à espera de ter um bocadinho para pegar no livro e mesmo nos capítulos sobre Daenerys - que é a parte menos interessante para mim - ficava absorvida logo após as primeiras</span>
  <span id="freeText13040256618615885114" style="display:none"><i>(review in english below)</i><br /><br />Adorei! <br />O autor revelou-se particularmente brilhante nesta parte da história, na forma como os personagens evoluem, no desenrolar dos acontecimentos, no modo como consegue manter-nos absolutamente suspensos, sem saber exactamente se as coisas são o que parecem...<br />Estive constantemente "agarrada", sempre à espera de ter um bocadinho para pegar no livro e mesmo nos capítulos sobre Daenerys - que é a parte menos interessante para mim - ficava absorvida logo após as primeiras linhas.<br />A descrição dos ambientes é muito boa e quando finalmente "assistimos" a uma batalha, não ficamos defraudados - as cenas desfilam na nossa mente à medida que são narradas com grande mestria.<br /><br />Entretanto já vi 4 episódios da 2ª temporada da série e as coisas começam a tornar-se um pouco confusas, não só porque a ordem dos acontecimentos é alterada mas também porque os próprios acontecimentos o são, além de serem introduzidas linhas narrativas que não existem nos livros, pelo menos nesta parte da história (é o caso de algumas sugestões de romance).<br /><br />Tinha pensado ler apenas, para já, os 4 primeiros livros, mas não me parece que consiga deixar esta história até ler tudo o que está publicado...<br /><br /><i>I loved it!<br />The author was particularly brilliant at writing this part of the story - the way the characters develop, the chain of events, how he keeps us completely hanging from his words, not knowing exactly if things are what they seem to be...<br />I was permanently hooked, always looking for a bit of free time to pick up the book and even the chapters about Danaerys - which I find the least interesting ones - grabbed me after the first couple of lines.<br />The ambience descriptions are excellent and when we finally witness a battle it doesn't let you down - the scenes unfold in your mind as they are masterfully narrated.<br /><br />Meanwhile I saw the first 4 episodes of the 2nd season and things are beginning to get a little confusing, because they altered not only the sequence of events but sometimes the events themselves. Also, the series has a few story lines that are not found in the books, at least in this part of the story, such as some romantic interests.<br /><br />I thought I'd read just the first 4 books (or the first original 2 books) for now, but I don't think I can walk away from this story until I read everything that was published so far...</i></span>

  <span id="freeText4525463758548414949" style="display:none">I really liked this second half of A Clash of Kings. It had some interesting twists and spins but also some predictable turns. I also liked the fact that it spends little time with my least favourite of all characters - Jon Snow - and that Sansa has stopped being so stupid.<br />I'm curious to see what will come out of the 3rd book (and 4th and 5th, I know). The only thing I missed was Tyrions sarcasm...for some reason he looses a bit of his wits once he becomes Hand of the King.<br />On the other hand I wished we had chapters in Lord Tywin Lannister's perspective (or Joffrey for that matter). The Lannisters are still my favourite House and I would like to understand better the characters.<br />Danny on the other hand was left with very little to do in this book. O tipo que a traduziu é um incompetente que revela uma profunda falta de controlo sobre a Língua Portuguesa.<br /><br />Fiz o apanhado de ALGUNS dos DISPARATES linguísticos cometidos que só revelam a profunda incapacidade do Sr. Candeias em dominar a língua Portuguesa (nem quero imaginar as atrocidades que escreve usando o Aborto Ortográfico...). Os que não estão aqui foi por não ter o telemóvel à mão quando estava a ler para os anotar.<br /><br />Pág.64<br />"Lisonjeaste‑los?", "Chorastes?". Ora bem, "Chorastes" estará bem conjugado se o personagem estiver a falar na 2ª pessoa do plural. Acontece que o Jorah estava a tratar a Danny na 2ª pessoa do singular. Logo o correcto seria "choraste?".<br />"Lisonjeaste‑los" é simplesmente espanholês. Em Português ou se diz "havei-los lisonjeado" ou "lisonjeaste-os". "Lisonjeaste-los" é simplesmente mau português.<br /><br />P.142 <br />"Poderia Dagmer ter ganhado". GANHADO? Eu gostava de saber é como é que este tipo conseguiu ter "ganhado" o emprego de tradutor. A professora dele não lhe deve ter ensinado que é "ganho" e não "ganhado" quando se reporta a acontecimentos do passado "Poderia Dagmer ter GANHO?"<br /><br />P.366 <br />"Queria perguntar se tinham ganhado a batalha".<br />E cá vamos nós outra vez.<br /><br />Eu acho é que os leitores portugueses já devem ter "ganhado" o Céu só por aturar tão más traduções por parte deste tipo. Santo Deus...</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13330278785565131859">Reasons why I loved this book: things happened. <br/>Reasons why I hated this book: things happened. <br/><br/>First of all, I've got to say this (more like repeat it), George R.R. Martin is just a genius.   <span id="freeText13330278785565131859" style="display:none">Reasons why I loved this book: things happened. <br />Reasons why I hated this book: things happened. <br /><br />First of all, I've got to say this (more like repeat it), George R.R. Martin is just a genius. His writting is absolutley amazing and the world he creates through the books is so amazingly well-conceived. <br /><br />My favourite main characters on this book were Tyrion (I think I'm always going to love him) and Jon Snow. Tyrion because he's inteligent, shrewd, and even though everyone hates him, he keeps on his mission of saving the Kingdom. He never gives up and he's one of the most strongest characters ever. <br />Jon because he's brave and he proves(just like the Halfman) that you can be SOMEONE no matter where you come from, how you look or the things other people think of you. Also, Jon is very humane. And that humanity allied with his courage is an important weapon.<br /><br />I also loved the participation of Jaqen H'ghar (not only in this book, I always liked him but never knew quite well why) that killed for Arya and is a man of many mysteries, Qhorin Halfhand - that is also a strong lider and a very smart individual (oh my...I cried so much on the last Jon's chapter because of him)- and Osha that is loyal to the end (I think xD). <br /><br />Now: Bran, Theon and Sansa...what the fugg?! What's wrong with you people? <br />First of all Bran, how can't you understand a metaphor? Did you thought that the sea was actually going to reach Winterfell? -.-" I mean, for God sake's. <br />Theon...you're just a little bastard aren't you? So full of yourself, so "I get what I want, no matter what" type of people. I never liked you but now I just hope Robb cuts your head off. <br />Sansa...little cheater. I hate how you think you're a victim when actually you were the responsible for all the tragedies that are happening. Woman up, okay? Stop living on your little fairy tale and wake up: life is way more than cute songs and prince charmings. <br /><br />Why only four stars? The descriptions of the battles didn't work for me and also some characters annoyed so much that I had to leave the book for a while (again, this just proves the geniality of George Martin). <br /><br />I don't like to talk about the story itself because I hate to spoil, but I can say it's full of action, emotional scenes, thriller and surprises. So get ready, buckle up and dive in this amazing world. :)</span>

<div id="review_203748945" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/203748945" />
    <a title="James" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/381252-james"><img alt="James" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1201318736p2/381252.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/203748945?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="James" class="user" itemprop="url" name="James" href="/user/show/381252-james">James</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/11336309-a-clash-of-kings-pt-2">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer203748945" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5392523096734388598">I'm in complete awe of Martin's ability as a writer. He weaves a complex tale of multiple families, multiple kings, and multiple battles into a coherent, suspenseful narrative. With chapters written from the perspectives of major characters, I always found myself upset when one chapter ended because I knew that it would be many more chapters until I returned to that corner of the world. Yet, nearly every story is deeply compelling. I'm probably late to the party on this one, but Martin has to be</span>
  <span id="freeText5392523096734388598" style="display:none">I'm in complete awe of Martin's ability as a writer. He weaves a complex tale of multiple families, multiple kings, and multiple battles into a coherent, suspenseful narrative. With chapters written from the perspectives of major characters, I always found myself upset when one chapter ended because I knew that it would be many more chapters until I returned to that corner of the world. Yet, nearly every story is deeply compelling. I'm probably late to the party on this one, but Martin has to be the heir to Tolkien; his characters leap off of the page and are incredibly flawed and human. His command of bloodlines, locations, and histories is encyclopedic. <br /><br />I'm eager to tear through the next three volumes in this series, but I am also conscious that reading "A Song of Fire and Ice" is a great, great privilege, one that I'll never get back again, much like Larsson's Salander series or King's Gunslinger books. <br /><br />Highly, highly recommended, but start with the first book, Game of Thrones. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5392523096734388598" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10770614118121783282">Loved this book. I like the way the characters are evolving given their circumstances. The way George R.R. Martin writes from the point of view of the different characters keeps the book from becoming confusing given the many (too many in my opinion) characters. Nothing is black and white.   <span id="freeText10770614118121783282" style="display:none">Loved this book. I like the way the characters are evolving given their circumstances. The way George R.R. Martin writes from the point of view of the different characters keeps the book from becoming confusing given the many (too many in my opinion) characters. Nothing is black and white. Even the good characters do things where "the ends justify the means". My own little quibble is that too many of the likeable characters are killed off. I'm hoping in the next books my favorites stay alive because I don't want to read a book where I don't like anyone. Also, I'm glad I read this book on my Kindle because GRRM uses words I have never heard or seen before. I found myself constantly using the dictionary feature on the Kindle.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DdKDREaJNyaVQs4+zX3kk7/zHXTFqVx7fVwncOCbww5oJcGheKwN6dEMFRTLQmgRxWV7IH7Z6zl1xip4gcC4jQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Wl+8Y+DE1ic2f7GaOW+LZ3Ga0RKOVmJtgi+/I14H61A/qP6G3uHs6HIxarA/UAflCwy3RjUm1S+KtbIrP1yQ0w==')})
  }

Es geht auf eine Reise zwischen Himmel und Hölle – und um die Frage, ob es das alles überhaupt gibt. Eine Reise, die geprägt ist durch die Tollpatschigkeit, mit der sich der Tod durch die Welt der Lebenden bewegt, und Fragen wie: Muss der Tod pinkeln? Der Mann, der als Vorsitzender der Jungen Union in Bayern, als Generalsekretär der CSU und als Minister durch provokative, laute Wortmeldungen bundesweit für Aufmerksamkeit und Aufregung gesorgt hat, wird beweisen müssen, was er wirklich kann. Söder polarisiert, innerhalb wie außerhalb der CSU. Warum und wie er während seiner gesamten politischen Laufbahn immer wieder Konflikte gesucht und für sich entschieden hat – zuletzt das jahrelange Duell mit Horst Seehofer – beantworten die Autoren Roman Deininger und Uwe Ritzer ebenso, wie die Frage nach Söders politischer Arbeit jenseits des gleißenden Scheinwerferlichts.Söder, der aus kleinen Verhältnissen stammt und in Nürnberg großgeworden ist, hatte außer Edmund Stoiber kaum einen Förderer – aber zahlreiche erbitterte Gegner. Mit unbedingtem Machtwillen, strategischem Blick und fleißigem Netzwerken hat Söder seinen Aufstieg in der Politik gestaltet und alle Konkurrenten geschlagen. Deininger und Ritzer erklären, was diesen Mann antreibt, abgesehen vom ehrgeizigen Ziel, den Gipfel der Macht zu erklimmen, was ihn geprägt hat und was nun von ihm zu erwarten ist. Die breiden Autoren haben lange und intensiv im politischen und privaten Umfeld Söders recherchiert, mit Feinden und Freunden des Politikers, sowie den relevanten Protagonisten der bayerischen Politik und der CSU gesprochen. Sie zeichnen in dieser ersten Biographie Söders das differenzierte Bild eines modernen Politikertypus: ehrgeizig, ich-fixiert, lösungsorientiert, der das traditionelle politische Handwerk ebenso beherrscht wie die digitale Kommunikation mit den Wählern.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/346732.George_R_R_Martin">About George R.R. Martin</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/346732.George_R_R_Martin"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_111x148-e08b4682eea7088f8cdfd67c131d51cd.png);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/346732.George_R_R_Martin">George R.R. Martin
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
96,725
followers
</div>

</div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9122181792650441492">George Raymond Richard "R.R." Martin was born September 20, 1948, in Bayonne, New Jersey. His father was Raymond Collins Martin, a longshoreman, and his mother was Margaret Brady Martin. He has two sisters, Darleen Martin Lapinski and Janet Martin Patten. <br/><br/>Martin attended Mary Jane Donohoe School and Marist High School. He began writing very young, selling monster stories to other neighborhood chil</span>
  <span id="freeText9122181792650441492" style="display:none">George Raymond Richard "R.R." Martin was born September 20, 1948, in Bayonne, New Jersey. His father was Raymond Collins Martin, a longshoreman, and his mother was Margaret Brady Martin. He has two sisters, Darleen Martin Lapinski and Janet Martin Patten. <br /><br />Martin attended Mary Jane Donohoe School and Marist High School. He began writing very young, selling monster stories to other neighborhood children for pennies, dramatic readings included. Later he became a comic book fan and collector in high school, and began to write fiction for comic fanzines (amateur fan magazines). Martin's first professional sale was made in 1970 at age 21: "The Hero," sold to Galaxy, published in February, 1971 issue. Other sales followed. <br /><br />In 1970 Martin received a B.S. in Journalism from Northwestern University, Evanston, Illinois, graduating summa cum laude. He went on to complete a M.S. in Journalism in 1971, also from Northwestern. <br /><br />As a conscientious objector, Martin did alternative service 1972-1974 with VISTA, attached to Cook County Legal Assistance Foundation. He also directed chess tournaments for the Continental Chess Association from 1973-1976, and was a Journalism instructor at Clarke College, Dubuque, Iowa, from 1976-1978. He wrote part-time throughout the 1970s while working as a VISTA Volunteer, chess director, and teacher. <br /><br />In 1975 he married Gale Burnick. They divorced in 1979, with no children. Martin became a full-time writer in 1979. He was writer-in-residence at Clarke College from 1978-79. <br /><br />Moving on to Hollywood, Martin signed on as a story editor for Twilight Zone at CBS Television in 1986. In 1987 Martin became an Executive Story Consultant for Beauty and the Beast at CBS. In 1988 he became a Producer for Beauty and the Beast, then in 1989 moved up to Co-Supervising Producer. He was Executive Producer for Doorways, a pilot which he wrote for Columbia Pictures Television, which was filmed during 1992-93. <br /><br />Martin's present home is Santa Fe, New Mexico. He is a member of Science Fiction &amp; Fantasy Writers of America (he was South-Central Regional Director 1977-1979, and Vice President 1996-1998), and of Writers' Guild of America, West. <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://us.macmillan.com/author/georgerrmartin">http://us.macmillan.com/author/george...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9122181792650441492" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>

This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
